1.Create file index
---------------
HttpMethod : PUT
URL : http://localhost:9200/file
Payload:
{
"index" :{
    "number_of_shards" :8, 
    "number_of_replicas" : 1
    }
} 

Response:
{
  "acknowledged": true,
  "shards_acknowledged": true
}
2. Create file mapping
----------------
HttpMethod : POST
URL : http://localhost:9200/file/file/_mapping
Payload:
{
    "dynamic" : "strict",
    "_all" : {
        "enabled" : false
    },

3.Adding file data
---------------
To delete exiting data, if required
HttpMethod : POST
URL : http://localhost:9200/file/file/_delete_by_query
Request object :
{
 "query" : {
 	"match_all" : {}
 }
} 

Response object :
{
  "acknowledged": true
}
